## @exports

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@exports</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@exports &lt;moduleName&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>在 JSDoc3.3.0 或更高版本中，<code>&lt;moduleName&gt;</code> 可以包含 <code>module:</code> 前缀。在以前的版本中，必须忽略此前缀。</p>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@exports</code> 标签描述除由 JavaScript 模块的 <code>exports</code> 或 <code>module.exports</code> 属性外导出的任何内容。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在模块中，当使用特定的 <code>exports</code> 模块，<code>@exports</code> 标签是不需要。JSDoc 会自动识别出该对象的导出成员。同样，JSDoc 会自动识别中的 Node.js 模块特定的 <code>module.exports</code> 属性。</p>
<p>CommonJS 模块:</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * A module that says hello!</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@module</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> hello/world</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Node.js 模块:</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code <p>如果模块导出使用的是除 <code>exports</code> 或 <code>module.exports</code> 之外的其他方法方式，使用 <code>@exports</code> 标签来说明哪些成员用于导出。</p>
<p>AMD 模块导出一个对象：</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js ## @external

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@external</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@host</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@external &lt;nameOfExternal&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@external</code> 标记标识在当前包外部定义的类、命名空间或模块。通过使用此标记，可以将包的扩展记录到外部符号，也可以向包的用户提供有关外部符号的信息。还可以在任何其他 JSDoc 标记中引用外部符号的 namepath。</p>
<p>外部符号的 namepath 始终使用前缀 <code>external:</code>（例如，<code>{@link external:Foo}</code> 或 <code>@augments external:Foo</code>）。但是，可以从 <code>@external</code> 标记中省略此前缀。</p>
<p>注 意：只能在你的项目之外定义的最高级别的标识上添加 <code>@external</code> 标签，请参见“描述一个嵌套的外部标识”的例子。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>以下示例显示如何将内置字符串对象作为外部对象以及新的实例方法 <code>external:String#rot13</code> 进行文档记录。</p>
<p>记录添加到内置类的方法:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The built in string object.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @external String</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @see {@link https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/String|String}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Create a ROT13-encoded version of the string. Added by the `foo` package.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function external:String#rot13</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @example</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * var greeting = new String('hello world');</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * console.log( greeting.rot13() ); // uryyb jbeyq</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>下面的例子中描述一个新 <code>starfairy</code> 功能如何添加到外部的 <code>jQuery.fn</code> 命名空间。</p>
<p>描述的外部的命名空间：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The jQuery plugin namespace.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @external "jQuery.fn"</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @see {@link http://learn.jquery.com/plugins/|jQuery Plugins}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A jQuery plugin to make stars fly around your home page.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function external:"jQuery.fn".starfairy</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>在下面的例子中，<code>EncryptedRequest</code> 类被描述为内置的 <code>XMLHttpRequest</code> 类的子类。</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The built-in class for sending HTTP requests.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @external XMLHttpRequest</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @see https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/XMLHttpRequest</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Extends the built-in `XMLHttpRequest` class to send data encoded with a secret key.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @class EncodedRequest</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @extends external:XMLHttpRequest</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>只能将 <code>@external</code> 标签添加到项目定义的最外最顶层。在下面的例子中，描述的是外部的 <code>security.TLS</code> 类。其结果是，<code>@external</code> 标签是用来描述外部的 <code>external:security</code> 命名空间，而不是外部类 <code>external:security.TLS</code>。</p>
<p>记录一个嵌套的外部标识：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * External namespace for security-related classes.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @external security</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @see http://example.org/docs/security</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * External class that provides Transport Layer Security (TLS) encryption.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @class TLS</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @memberof external:security</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @file

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@file</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@fileoverview</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@overview</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@file &lt;descriptionOfFile&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@file</code> 标签提供文件的说明。在文件开头的 JSDoc 注释部分使用该标签。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>文件描述：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @file Manages the configuration settings for the widget.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @author Rowina Sanela </span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>

<li><a href="/tags-version">@version</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @fires

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@fires</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@emits</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@fires &lt;className&gt;#[event:]&lt;eventName&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@fires</code> 标记表示方法在调用时可以触发指定类型的事件。使用 <a href="/tags-event">@event</a>标记来记录事件的内容。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>方法将触发 "drain" 事件：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Drink the milkshake.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @fires Milkshake#drain</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">Milkshake.prototype.drink = function() {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  // ...</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">};</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-event">@event</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-listens">@listens</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @function

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@function</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@func</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@method</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@function [&lt;functionName&gt;]</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>将一个对象标记为一个函数，即使在解析器看来它可能不是一个函数。它将 doclet 的 <a href="/tags-kind">@kind</a> 设置为 <code>'function'</code>。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@function</code> 标记为一个函数：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @function */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var paginate = paginateFactory(pages);</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>如果没有 <code>@function</code> 标记，<code>paginate</code> 对象将被记录为泛型对象（一个 <a href="/tags-member">@member</a>），因为从检查代码行中无法判断 <code>paginate</code> 在运行时将保存哪种类型的值。</p>
<p>使用带函数名的 <code>@function</code>：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @function myFunction */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// the above is the same as:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @function</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @name myFunction </span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-kind">@kind</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-member">@member</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-name">@name</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @generator

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@generator</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@generator</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@generator</code> 标记表示函数是一个生成器函数，这意味着它是使用语法函数 <code>*foo () {}</code> 声明的。JSDoc 3.5.0 及更高版本中提供了此标记。</p>
<p>一般来说，不需要使用此标记，因为 JSDoc 会自动检测生成器函数并在生成的文档中标识它们。但是，如果您正在为代码中没有出现的生成器函数编写虚拟注释，则可以使用此标记告诉 JSDoc 该函数是生成器函数。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>以下示例显示使用 <code>@generator</code> 标记的虚拟注释。</p>
<p>带有 <code>@generator</code> 标记的虚拟注释:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Generate numbers in the Fibonacci sequence.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @generator</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function fibonacci</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @yields {number} The next number in the Fibonacci sequence.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @global

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@global</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@global</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@global</code> 标记指定一个符号应作为全局符号出现在文档中。JSDoc 忽略源文件中符号的实际作用域。此标记对于在本地定义然后指定给全局符号的符号特别有用。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@global</code> 标签来指定一个标识应记录为全局。</p>
<p>将内部变量记录为全局变量:</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-javascript codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/** </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@global</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">var</span><span class="token plain"> foo </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">'hello foo'</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">foo</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> foo</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token method function property-access" style="color:#d73a49">apply</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token dom variable" style="color:#36acaa">window</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-inner">@inner</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-instance">@instance</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-memberof">@memberof</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-static">@static</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @hideconstructor

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@hideconstructor</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@hideconstructor</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@hideconstructor</code> 标记告诉 JSDoc 生成的文档不应该显示类的构造函数。JSDoc 3.5.0 及更高版本中提供了此标记。</p>
<p>对于 ES2015 之前的类，请将此标记与 <a href="/tags-class">@class</a> 或 <a href="/tags-class">@constructor</a>标记结合使用。</p>
<p>对于 ES2015 类，请在构造函数的 JSDoc 注释中使用此标记。如果类没有显式构造函数，请在类的 JSDoc 注释中使用此标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>ES2015 之前的类带有 <code>@hideconstructor</code>:</p>

plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">if</span><span class="token </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">return</span><span class="token plain"> #instance</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span ## @ignore

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@ignore</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@ignore</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@ignore</code> 标签表示在代码中的注释不应该出现在文档中，注释会被直接忽略。这个标签优先于所有其他标签。</p>
<p>对于大多数 JSDoc 模板来说，包括默认模板，<code>@ignore</code> 标签具有以下效果：</p>
<ul>
<li>如果您和 <a href="/tags-class">@class</a> 或 <a href="/tags-module">@module</a> 标签结合使用 <code>@ignore</code> 标签，整个类或模块的 JSDoc 注释文档会被省略。</li>
<li>如果您和 <a href="/tags-namespace">@namespace</a> 标签结合使用 <code>@ignore</code> 标签，必须将 <code>@ignore</code> 标签添加到任意子类和命名空间中。否则，会显示子类和命名空间的文档，但不完整。</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在下面的例子中，<code>Jacket</code> 和 <code>Jacket#color</code> 将不会出现在文档中。</p>
<p>在 Class 中使用 <code>@ignore</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @class</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @ignore</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function Jacket() {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  /** The jacket's color. */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  this.color = null;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>在下面的例子中， <code>Clothes</code> 命名空间包含一个 <code>Jacket</code> 类。<code>@ignore</code> 标签必须添加到 <code>Clothes</code> 和 <code>Clothes.Jacket</code> 中。<code>Clothes</code>, <code>Clothes.Jacket</code> 和 <code>Clothes.Jacket#color</code> 将不会出现在文档。</p>
<p>带子类的命名空间：</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-javascript codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@namespace</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@ignore</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">var</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token maybe-class-name">Clothes</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@ignore</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token function-variable function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Jacket</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/** The jacket's color. */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">color</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword null nil" style="color:#00009f">null</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @implements

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@implements</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@implements {typeExpression}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@implements</code> 标签表示一个标识实现一个接口。</p>
<p>添加 <code>@implements</code> 标签到实现接口（例如，一个构造函数）的顶层标识。不需要将 <code>@implements</code> 标签添加到实现接口（例如，实现的实例方法）的每个成员上。</p>
<p>如果没有在实现的接口中描述这个标识，JSDoc 会自动使用该接口文档的标识。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在下面的例子中，<code>TransparentColor</code> 类实现 <code>Color</code> 接口，并添加了 <code>TransparentColor#rgba</code> 方法。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@implements</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-javascript codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Interface for classes that represent a color.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@interface</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Color</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Get the color as an array of red, green, and blue values, represented as</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * decimal numbers between 0 and 1.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@returns</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">Array</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">&lt;</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">number</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">&gt;</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> An array containing the red, green, and blue values,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * in that order.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token class-name">Color</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">prototype</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token method-variable function-variable method function property-access" style="color:#d73a49">rgb</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token implemented"</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Class representing a color with transparency information.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@implements</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">Color</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" ## @inheritdoc

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@inheritdoc</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@inheritdoc</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@inheritdoc</code> 标记表示应该从其父类继承其文档。JSDoc 注释中包含的任何其他标记都将被忽略。</p>
<p>提供此标记是为了与 <a href="https://developers.google.com/closure/compiler/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Closure Compiler</a> 兼容。默认情况下，如果不向符号添加 JSDoc 注释，标识符将从其父级继承文档。</p>
<p><code>@inheritdoc</code> 标记的存在意味着 <a href="/tags-override">@override</a> 标记的存在。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>下面的例子显示了一个类的描述如何从它的父类继承文档。</p>
<p>一个类继承自他的父类：</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Abstract class representing a network connection.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Connection</span><span class="token punctuation" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Open the connection.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span><span class="token punctuation" */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Socket</span><span class="token punctuation" ## @inner

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@inner</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@inner</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@inner</code> 标记会将符号标记为其父符号的内部成员。这意味着它可以被 <code>“Parent~Child”</code> 引用。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@inner</code> 将覆盖 doclet 的默认作用域（除非它在全局作用域中，在这种情况下它将保持全局作用域）。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@inner</code> 使一个虚拟的 doclet 作为内部成员：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @namespace MyNamespace */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * myFunction is now MyNamespace~myFunction.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function myFunction</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @memberof MyNamespace</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @inner</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>注意，在上面的代码我们也可以使用 <code>"@function MyNamespace~myFunction"</code>，代替 <a href="/tags-memberof">@memberof</a>和 <code>@inner</code> 标签。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@inner</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @namespace */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var MyNamespace = {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  /**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   * foo is now MyNamespace~foo rather than MyNamespace.foo.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   * @inner</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  foo: 1</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">};</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>在上面的例子中，我们使用 <code>@inner</code> 迫使一个命名空间的成员被描述作为内部成员（默认情况下，这是一个静态成员）。这意味着，<code>foo</code> 现在有了 <code>MyNamespace~foo</code> 新名字，而不是 <code>MyNamespace.foo</code>。</p>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-global">@global</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-instance">@instance</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-static">@static</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @instance

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@instance</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@instance</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@instance</code> 标记会将符号标记为其父符号的实例成员。这意味着它可以被称为 <code>Parent#Child</code>。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@instance</code> 将覆盖 doclet 的默认作用域（除非它在全局作用域中，在这种情况下，它将保持全局作用域）。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>下面的例子是 <code>@function MyNamespace#myFunction</code> 的一个普通写法。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@instance</code> 使一个虚拟的 doclet 作为实例成员:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @namespace MyNamespace */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * myFunction is now MyNamespace#myFunction.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function myFunction</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @memberof MyNamespace</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @instance</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>更有用的是，可以使用 <code>@instance</code> 标记覆盖 JSDoc 推断的范围。例如，可以指示静态成员用作实例成员。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@instance</code> 标识实例成员:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @namespace */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var BaseObject = {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  /**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   * foo is now BaseObject#foo rather than BaseObject.foo.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   * @instance</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">   */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  foo: null</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">};</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** Generates BaseObject instances. */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function fooFactory(fooValue) {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  var props = { foo: fooValue };</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  return Object.create(BaseObject, props);</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-global">@global</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-inner">@inner</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-static">@static</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @interface

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@interface</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<p>用作 JSDoc 标签字典 (默认开启):</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@interface [&lt;name&gt;]</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>用作 Closure Compiler 标签字典:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@interface</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@interface</code> 标签使一个标识符作为其他标识符的一个实现接口。 例如，你的代码可能定义一个父类，它的方法和属性被去掉。您可以将 <code>@interface</code> 标签添加到父类，以指明子类必须实现父类的方法和属性。</p>
<p>作为接口，<code>@interface</code> 标记应该添加到顶层标识符（例如，一个构造函数）。你并不需要将 <code>@interface</code> 标签添加加到实现接口（例如，实现的实例方法）的每个成员上。</p>
<p>如果您使用的是 JSDoc 标记字典（默认启用），你还可以定  义一个接口的虚拟注释，而不是为接口编写代码。见一个例子“定义一个接口的虚拟注释”。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在下面的例子中，<code>Color</code> 函数表示其它类可以实现的接口。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@interface</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Interface for classes that represent a color.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @interface</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function Color() {}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Get the color as an array of red, green, and blue values, represented as</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * decimal numbers between 0 and 1.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @returns {Array&lt;number&gt;} An array containing the red, green, and blue values,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * in that order.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">Color.prototype.rgb = function() {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  throw new Error('not implemented');</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">};</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>下面的例子使用虚拟注释，而不是代码，来定义 <code>Color</code> 接口。</p>
<p>虚拟注释来定义一个接口：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Interface for classes that represent a color.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @interface Color</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Get the color as an array of red, green, and blue values, represented as</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * decimal numbers between 0 and 1.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @name Color#rgb</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @returns {Array&lt;number&gt;} An array containing the red, green, and blue values,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * in that order.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-implements">@implements</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @kind

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@kind</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@kind &lt;kindName&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>&lt;kindName&gt;</code> 取值为：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>class</code></li>
<li><code>constant</code></li>
<li><code>event</code></li>
<li><code>external</code></li>
<li><code>file</code></li>
<li><code>function</code></li>
<li><code>member</code></li>
<li><code>mixin</code></li>
<li><code>module</code></li>
<li><code>namespace</code></li>
<li><code>typedef</code></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@kind</code> 标签是用来指明什么样的标识符被描述（例如，一类或模块）。标识符 <code>kind</code> 不同于标识符 <code>type</code>（例如，字符串或布尔）。</p>
<p>通常你不需要 <code>@kind</code> 标签，因为标识符的 <code>kind</code> 是由 doclet 的其他标记来确定。例如，使用 <a href="/tags-class">@class</a> 标签自动意味着 <code>@kind class</code>，使用 <a href="/tags-namespace">@namespace</a> 标签则意味着 <code>@kind namespace</code>。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@kind</code>：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// The following examples produce the same result:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A constant.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @kind constant</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">const asdf = 1;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A constant.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @constant</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">const asdf = 1;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>kind</code> 标签可能引起冲突（例如，使用 <a href="/tags-module">@module</a>，表示他的 <code>kind</code> 为 <code>module</code>，同时，又使用了 <code>@kind constant</code>，表示他的 <code>kind</code> 为 <code>constant</code>），在这种情况下最后的标签决定 <code>kind</code> 的值。</p>
<p>冲突的 <code>@kind</code> 语句：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * This will show up as a constant</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @module myModule</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @kind constant</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * This will show up as a module.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @kind constant</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @module myModule</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-type">@type</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @lends

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@lends</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@lends &lt;namepath&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@lends</code> 标签允许将一个字面量对象的所有成员标记为某个标识符的成员，就像他们是给定名称的标识符成员。如果要将对象文字传递给从其成员创建命名类的函数，则可能需要执行此操作。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在本例中，我们希望使用一个 <code>helper</code> 函数来创建一个名为 <code>Person</code> 的类，以及名为 <code>initialize</code> 和 <code>say</code> 的实例方法。这与一些流行的框架处理类创建的方式类似。</p>
<p>示例类:</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-javascript codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// We want to document this as being a class</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">var</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token maybe-class-name">Person</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">makeClass</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// We want to document these as being methods</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token function-variable function" style="color:#d73a49">initialize</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token function-variable function" style="color:#d73a49">say</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">message</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">return</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">+</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">" says: "</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">+</span><span class="token plain"> message</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>如果没有任何注释，JSDoc 将无法识别这段代码使用两个方法创建一个 <code>Person</code> 类。要记录这些方法，我们必须在 doc 注释中紧靠对象文本之前使用 <code>@lends</code> 标记。<code>@lends</code> 标记告诉 JSDoc，该对象文本的所有成员名称都被“借用”给一个名为 <code>Person</code> 的变量。我们还必须为每种方法添加注释。</p>
<p>下面的例子让我们更接近我们想要的：</p>

<p>现在名为 <code>initialize</code> 和 <code>say</code> 的函数会被文档化，但它们被标记为 <code>Person</code> 类的静态方法。这可能是你期望的，但有种情况下我们想要 <code>initialize</code> 和 <code>say</code> 属于 <code>Person</code> 类的实例。所以，我们通过少做改动,使其成为原型的方法。</p>
<p>标记为实例方法:</p>

<p>最后一步：我们的类框架使用借出的 <code>initialize</code> 函数来构造 <code>Person</code> 实例，但是 <code>Person</code> 实例没有自己的 <code>initialize</code> 方法。解决方案是将 <code>@constructs</code> 标记添加到借出的函数中。记住也要删除 <code>@class</code> 标记，否则会记录两个类。</p>
<p>与构造器一起记录:</p>

class="token function-variable function" style="color:#d73a49">initialize</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">name</span><span class="token punctuation" ## @license

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@license</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@license &lt;identifier&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@license</code> 标记标识应用于代码任何部分的软件许可证。</p>
<p>您可以使用任何文本来标识正在使用的许可证。如果代码使用标准的开源许可证，请考虑使用<a href="https://spdx.org/licenses/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">the Software Package Data Exchange (SPDX) License List</a>中的相应标识符。</p>
<p>一些 JavaScript 处理工具，比如 Google 的 Closure 编译器，会自动保存任何包含 <code>@license</code> 标记的 JSDoc 注释。如果您正在使用其中一个工具，您可能希望添加一个独立的 JSDoc 注释，该注释包括 <code>@license</code> 标记以及许可证的整个文本，以便许可证文本将包含在生成的JavaScript 文件中。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在Apache 2.0 许可下分发的模块：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Utility functions for the foo package.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @module foo/util</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @license Apache-2.0</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>一个独立的 JSDoc 注释块，包含完整的MIT许可:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Permission is hereby granted, free of charge, to any person obtaining a copy</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * of this software and associated documentation files (the "Software"), to deal</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * in the Software without restriction, including without limitation the rights</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * to use, copy, modify, merge, publish, distribute, sublicense, and/or sell</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * copies of the Software, and to permit persons to whom the Software is</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * furnished to do so, subject to the following conditions:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The above copyright notice and this permission notice shall be included in all</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * copies or substantial portions of the Software.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * THE SOFTWARE IS PROVIDED "AS IS", WITHOUT WARRANTY OF ANY KIND, EXPRESS OR</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * IMPLIED, INCLUDING BUT NOT LIMITED TO THE WARRANTIES OF MERCHANTABILITY,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE AND NONINFRINGEMENT. IN NO EVENT SHALL THE</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * AUTHORS OR COPYRIGHT HOLDERS BE LIABLE FOR ANY CLAIM, DAMAGES OR OTHER</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * LIABILITY, WHETHER IN AN ACTION OF CONTRACT, TORT OR OTHERWISE, ARISING FROM,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * OUT OF OR IN CONNECTION WITH THE SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN THE</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * SOFTWARE.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @listens

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@listens</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@listens &lt;eventName&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@listens</code> 标记指示符号侦听指定的事件。使用 <a href="/tags-event">@event</a>标记来记录事件的内容。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>下面的示例演示了如何记录名为 <code>module:hurler~event:snowball</code> 的事件，还有一个方法命名为 <code>module:playground/monitor.reportThrowage</code> 来监听事件。</p>
<p>描述一个事件和它的监听器:</p>
