<li><a href="/tags-static">@static</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @public

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@public</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@public</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@public</code> 标签标记标识符为公开的。</p>
<p>默认情况下，JSDoc 把所有标识符当做公开的，因此使用这个标记一般不会影响生成的文档。 然而，你可能更愿意明确地使用 <code>@public</code> 标签，这样可以更加清晰的标明你要公开的标识符。</p>
<p>在 JSDoc3 中，<code>@public</code> 标签不影响标识符的作用域。使用 <a href="/tags-instance">@instance</a>, <a href="/tags-static">@static</a>, 和 <a href="/tags-global">@global</a> 标签会改变标识符的作用域。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@public</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * The Thingy class is available to all.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@public</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Thingy</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   * The Thingy~foo member. Note that 'foo' is still an inner member</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   * of 'Thingy', in spite of the @public tag.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@public</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">var</span><span class="token plain"> foo </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-access">@access</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-global">@global</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-instance">@instance</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-package">@package</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-private">@private</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-protected">@protected</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-static">@static</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @readonly

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@readonly</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@readonly</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>标记一个标识符为只读。JSDoc 不会检查某个代码是否真是只读的，只要标上 <code>@readonly</code>，在文档中就体现为只读的。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@readonly</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A constant.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @readonly</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @const {number}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">const FOO = 1;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>带有 <code>@readonly</code> 标签的 <code>getter</code>:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js Plain.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   */</span><span class="token style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">   */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">" with ice cream"</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span ## @requires

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@requires</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@requires &lt;someModuleName&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@requires</code> 标签可以记录一个模块需要的依赖项。一个 JSDoc 注释块可以有多个 <code>@require</code> 标签。模块名可以被指定为 "moduleName" 或者 "module:moduleName";这两种形式将被解析为模块。</p>
<p>JSDoc 不会尝试处理被包含的模块。如果您希望该模块包含到文档中，您必须将模块包含到 JavaScript 文件列表进行处理。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@requires</code> 标签:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * This class requires the modules </span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@link</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> module:xyzcorp/helper</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> and</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@link</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> module:xyzcorp/helper.ShinyWidget#polish</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@requires</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> module:xyzcorp/helper</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@requires</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> xyzcorp/helper.ShinyWidget#polish</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Widgetizer</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @returns

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@returns</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@return</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@return [{type}] [description]</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@returns</code> 标记记录函数返回的值。</p>
<p>如果要记录生成器函数，请使用 <a href="/tags-yields">@yiels</a> 标记而不是此标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>返回值的类型:</p>

style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">boolean</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> If set to true, the function will return an array</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@returns</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">(</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">number</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name operator" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">|</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">Array</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">)</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Sum of a and b or an array that contains a, b and the sum of a and b.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">sum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">a</span><span class="token parameter punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token parameter"> b</span><span class="token parameter punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token parameter"> retArr</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">return</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token <p>返回 <code>Promise</code>:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@returns</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" ## @see

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@see</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@see &lt;namepath&gt;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@see &lt;text&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@see</code> 标签表示可以参考另一个标识符的说明文档，或者一个外部资源。您可以提供一个标识符的 <code>namepath</code> 或自由格式的文本。如果你提供了一个 <code>namepath</code>，JSDoc 的默认模板会自动将 <code>namepath</code> 转换成链接。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@see</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Both of these will link to the bar function.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@see</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">@link bar</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@see</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> bar</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">foo</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// Use the inline {@link} tag to include a link within a free-form description.</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@see</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">@link foo</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> for further information.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@see</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment operator" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">|</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">GitHub</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">bar</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>

## @since

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@since</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@since &lt;versionDescription&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@since</code> 标记表示在特定版本中添加了类、方法或其他符号。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@since</code>:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Provides access to user information.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@since</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> 1.0.1</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">UserRecord</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>

## @static

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@static</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@static</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@static</code> 标记表示符号包含在父项中，可以在不实例化父项的情况下访问。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@static</code> 标记将覆盖符号的默认作用域，但有一个例外：全局作用域中的符号将保持全局。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>下面的例子可以写成 <code>"@function MyNamespace.myFunction"</code> 并省略 <code>@memberof</code> 和 <code>@static</code> 标签，他们的效果是一样的.</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @namespace MyNamespace */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @function myFunction</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @memberof MyNamespace</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @static</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>下面的示例强制模块的内部成员被描述为静态成员。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@static</code> 来覆盖默认作用域：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @module Rollerskate */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The 'wheel' variable is documented as Rollerskate.wheel</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * rather than Rollerskate~wheel.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @static</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var wheel = 1;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-global">@global</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-inner">@inner</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-instance">@instance</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @summary

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@summary</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@summary Summary goes here.</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@summary</code> 标签是完整描述的一个简写版本。它可以被添加到任何的 doclet。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A very long, verbose, wordy, long-winded, tedious, verbacious, tautological,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * profuse, expansive, enthusiastic, redundant, flowery, eloquent, articulate,</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * loquacious, garrulous, chatty, extended, babbling description.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @summary A concise summary.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function bloviate() {}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @this

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@this</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@this &lt;namePath&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@this</code> 标签指明 <code>this</code> 关键字的指向。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在下面的例子中，<code>@this</code> 标签迫使 <code>"this.name"</code> 被描述为 <code>"Greeter#name"</code>，而不是全局变量 <code>"name"</code>。</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function maybe-class-name" style="color:#d73a49">Greeter</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  setName</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token method function property-access" style="color:#d73a49">apply</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/** </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@this</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">Greeter</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">setName</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/** document me */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">this</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @throws

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@throws</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@exception</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@throws free-form description</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@throws {&lt;type&gt;}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@throws {&lt;type&gt;} free-form description</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@throws</code> 标记记录函数可能引发的错误。可以在一个 JSDoc 注释中多次包含 <code>@throws</code> 标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用带有类型的 <code>@throws</code> 标记:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@throws</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">InvalidArgumentException</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">foo</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">x</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>使用带有描述的 <code>@throws</code> 标记:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@throws</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Will throw an error if the argument is null.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">bar</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">x</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>使用带有类型和描述的 <code>@throws</code> 标记:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@throws</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Argument x must be non-zero.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">baz</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">x</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" ## @todo

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@todo</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@todo text describing thing to do.</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@todo</code> 标签记录要完成的任务。在一个 JSDoc 注释块中您可以包含多个 <code>@todo</code> 标签。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@todo</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@todo</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Write the documentation.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@todo</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Implement this function.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">foo</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// write me</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div>

## @tutorial

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@tutorial</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@tutorial &lt;tutorialID&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@tutorial</code> 标签插入一个指向向导教程的链接，作为文档的一部分。有关创建教程指导请参阅 <a href="/about-tutorials">tutorials overview</a>。</p>
<p>可以在一个 JSDoc 注释中多次使用 <code>@tutorial</code> 标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>在下面的示例中，<code>MyClass</code> 的文档将链接到具有标识符 <code>tutorial-1</code> 和 <code>tutorial-2</code> 的教程。</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Description</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @class</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @tutorial tutorial-1</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @tutorial tutorial-2</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function MyClass() {}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/about-tutorials">Tutorials</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-inline-tutorial">{@tutorial}</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-see">@see</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @type

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@type</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@type {typeName}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@type</code> 标记允许您提供一个类型表达式，用于标识符号可能包含的值类型或函数返回的值类型。您还可以将类型表达式包含在许多其他 JSDoc 标记中，比如 <a href="/tags-param">@param</a> 标记。</p>
<p>类型表达式可以包括符号的 JSDoc namepath（例如，<code>myNamespace.MyClass</code>）、内置的 JavaScript 类型（例如，string）或它们的组合。您可以使用任何 Google Closure Compiler 编译器类型表达式，以及特定于JSDoc的其他几种格式。</p>
<p>如果 JSDoc 确定类型表达式无效，它将显示错误并停止运行。通过使用 <code>--lenient</code> 选项运行 JSDoc，可以将此错误转换为警告。</p>
<p>注意：JSDoc 3.2 和更高版本中完全支持 Google Closure Compiler 编译器样式的类型表达式。JSDoc 的早期版本包括对闭包编译器类型表达式的部分支持。</p>
<p>通过使用下面描述的格式之一提供类型表达式来指定每个类型。在适当的情况下，JSDoc 将自动为其他符号创建指向文档的链接。例如，如果该符号已被文档化，<code>@type {MyClass}</code>将链接到 <code>MyClass</code> 文档。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="symbol-name-name-expression">Symbol name (name expression)</h3>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{boolean}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{myNamespace.MyClass}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>指定符号的名称。如果标识符已经被文档化，JSDoc 将创建一个链接到该标识符的文档。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="multiple-types-type-union">Multiple types (type union)</h3>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{(number|boolean)}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>这意味着值可能是几种类型中的一种，用括号括起来，并用"|"分隔类型的完整列表。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="arrays-and-objects-type-applications-and-record-types">Arrays and objects (type applications and record types)</h3>
<p>MyClass的实例的数组:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{Array.&lt;MyClass&gt;}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// or:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{MyClass[]}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>具有字符串键和数值的对象：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{Object.&lt;string, number&gt;}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>名为 <code>myObj</code> 的对象，属性为“a”（数字）、“b”（字符串）和“c”（任何类型）:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{{a: number, b: string, c}} myObj</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// or:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{Object} myObj</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{number} myObj.a</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{string} myObj.b</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{*} myObj.c</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>JSDoc 支持 Closure Compiler 语法定义的数组和对象类型。</p>
<p>还可以通过数组后面附加<code>[]</code>指示包含在数组中的类型。例如，表达式<code>string[]</code>表示字符串数组。</p>
<p>对于具有一组已知的属性的对象，你可以使用 Closure Compiler 语法文档化标注的类型。也可以分别描述每个属性，这使您能够提供有关每个属性的更多详细信息。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="nullable-type">Nullable type</h3>
<p>一个数字或空值：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{?number}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>指明类型为指定的类型，或者为 <code>null</code>。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="non-nullable-type">Non-nullable type</h3>
<p>一个数字，但是绝对不会是 <code>null</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{!number}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>指明类型为指定的类型，但是绝对不会是 <code>null</code>。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="variable-number-of-that-type">Variable number of that type</h3>
<p>此函数接受可变数量的数值参数:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@param {...number} num</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>指示函数接受可变数目的参数，并指定参数的类型。例如：</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * Returns the sum of all numbers passed to the function.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@param</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name operator" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">...</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">number</span><span class="token doc-comment comment class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> </span><span class="token doc-comment comment parameter" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">num</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> A positive or negative number</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">sum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">num</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">var</span><span class="token plain"> i</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> n</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain">arguments</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token property-access">length</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> t</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">for</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"> i</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token plain">n</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"> i</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">++</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    t </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">+=</span><span class="token plain"> arguments</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain">i</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword control-flow" style="color:#00009f">return</span><span class="token plain"> t</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="optional-parameter">Optional parameter</h3>
<p>一个可选参数 <code>foo</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@param {number} [foo]</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// or:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@param {number=} foo</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>一个可选参数 <code>foo</code>，默认值为 <code>1</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@param {number} [foo=1]</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>表示该参数是可选的。当对可选参数使用 JSDoc 的语法时，还可以显示在省略参数时将使用的值。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="callbacks">Callbacks</h3>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @callback myCallback</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @param {number} x - ...</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @type {myCallback} */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var cb;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>使用 <code>@callback</code> 标签指明一个回调。和 <code>@typedef</code> 标签是相同的，不同之处在于回调的类型始终是"function"。</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorWithStickyNavbar_LWe7" id="type-definitions">Type definitions</h3>
<p>记录 <code>id</code>, <code>name</code>, <code>age</code> 属性的类型：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @typedef PropertiesHash</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @type {object}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {string} id - an ID.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {string} name - your name.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {number} age - your age.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @type {PropertiesHash} */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var props;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>您可以使用 <code>@typedef</code> 标签记录复杂类型，然后参考类型定义在你文档的其他地方。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @type {(string|Array.)} */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var foo;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @type {number} */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var bar = 1;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>在许多情况下，您可以包含一个类型表达式作为另一个标签的一部分，而不是在 JSDoc 注释块中包含独立 <code>@type</code> 标签。</p>
<p>类型表达式可以有多个标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @type {number}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @const</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var FOO = 1;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">// same as:</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/** @const {number} */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">var FOO = 1;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-callback">@callback</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-typedef">@typedef</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-param">@param</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-property">@property</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @typedef

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@typedef</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@typedef [&lt;type&gt;] &lt;namepath&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@typedef</code> 标签在描述自定义类型时是很有用的，特别是如果你要反复引用它们的时候。这些类型可以在其它标签内使用，如 <code>@type</code> 和 <code>@param</code>。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@callback</code> 标签表明回调函数的类型。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>这个例子定义了一个联合类型的参数，表示可以包含数字或字符串。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@typedef</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A number, or a string containing a number.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @typedef {(number|string)} NumberLike</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Set the magic number.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @param {NumberLike} x - The magic number.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function setMagicNumber(x) {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>这个例子定义了一个更复杂的类型，一个具有多个属性的对象，并设置了它的 <code>namepath</code>，这样它将与使用该类型的类一起显示。因为类型定义实际上不是由类公开的，所以通常将类型定义记录为内部成员。</p>
<p>使用 <code>@typedef</code> 记录类的复杂类型:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * The complete Triforce, or one or more components of the Triforce.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @typedef {Object} WishGranter~Triforce</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {boolean} hasCourage - Indicates whether the Courage component is present.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {boolean} hasPower - Indicates whether the Power component is present.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @property {boolean} hasWisdom - Indicates whether the Wisdom component is present.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * A class for granting wishes, powered by the Triforce.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @class</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @param {...WishGranter~Triforce} triforce - One to three {@link WishGranter~Triforce} objects</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * containing all three components of the Triforce.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function WishGranter(triforce) {}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-callback">@callback</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-param">@param</a></li>
<li><a href="/tags-type">@type</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @variation

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@variation</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@variation &lt;variationNumber&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p>有时代码可能包含多个具有相同长名称的符号。例如，您可能同时拥有一个全局类和一个名为 <code>Widget</code> 的顶级命名空间。在这种情况下，<code>{@link Widget}</code> 或 <code>@memberof Widget</code> 是什么意思？全局命名空间，还是全局类？</p>
<p>变体有助于 JSDoc 区分具有相同长名称的不同符号。例如，如果将 <code>“@variation 2”</code> 添加到小部件类的JSDoc注释中，<code>“{@link Widget(2)}”</code> 将引用该类，<code>“{@link Widget}”</code> 将引用命名空间。或者，当您使用诸如 <code>@alias</code> 或 <code>@name</code> 之类的标记（例如，<code>“@alias Widget(2)”</code>）指定符号时，也可以包含变体。</p>
<p>您可以使用 <code>@variation</code> 标记提供任何值，只要该值和 longname 的组合产生了 longname 的全局唯一版本。作为最佳实践，使用可预测的模式来选择值，这将使您更容易编写代码文档。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>下面的示例使用 <code>@variation</code> 标签来区分 <code>Widget</code> 类和 <code>Widget</code> 命名空间。</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * The Widget namespace.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@namespace</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Widget</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// you can also use '@class Widget(2)' and omit the @variation tag</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * The Widget class. Defaults to the properties in </span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@link</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> Widget.properties</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@class</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line"
