## @version

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@version</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@version &lt;version&gt;</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@version</code> 标签后面的文本将被用于表示该项的版本。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>使用 <code>@version</code> 标签：</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Solves equations of the form a * x = b. Returns the value</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * of x.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @version 1.2.3</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @tutorial solver</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function solver(a, b) {</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  return b / a;</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-since">@since</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @yields

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@yields</h1>
<h2 id="别名">别名</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@yield</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">@yields [{type}] [description]</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>@yields</code> 标记记录生成器函数生成的值。JSDoc 3.5.0 及更高版本中提供了此标记。</p>
<p>如果要记录常规函数，请使用 <a href="/tags-returns">@returns</a> 标记而不是此标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>带有类型的 <code>@yields</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Generate the Fibonacci sequence of numbers.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @yields {number}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function* fibonacci() {}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>带有类型和描述的 <code>@yields</code>:</p>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">/**</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * Generate the Fibonacci sequence of numbers.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> *</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> * @yields {number} The next number in the Fibonacci sequence.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> */</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">function* fibonacci() {}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="相关链接">相关链接</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/tags-returns">@returns</a></li>
</ul></div>

## @tutorial

<div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><h1>@tutorial</h1>
<h2 id="语法">语法</h2>
<div class="codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa" tabindex="0"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{@tutorial tutorialID}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">[link text]{@tutorial tutorialID}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{@tutorial tutorialID|link text}</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{@tutorial tutorialID link text (after the first space)}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><code>{@tutorial}</code> 内联标记创建指向您指定的教程标识符的链接。使用 <code>{@tutorial}</code> 标记时，还可以使用几种不同格式之一提供链接文本。如果不提供任何链接文本，JSDoc 将使用教程的标题作为链接文本。</p>
<p>如果需要链接到 <code>namepath</code> 或 <code>URL</code>，请使用 <a href="/tags-inline-link">{@link}</a>内联标记，而不是 <code>{@tutorial}</code> 标记。</p>
<h2 id="实例">实例</h2>
<p>以下示例显示了为 <code>{@tutorial}</code> 标记提供链接文本的所有方法。</p>
<p>提供链接文本:</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code language-js keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@tutorial</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> gettingstarted</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> and [Configuring the Dashboard]</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@tutorial</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> dashboard</span><span class="token doc-comment comment style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * For more information, see </span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@tutorial</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> create|Creating a Widget</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> and</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> * </span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">{</span><span class="token doc-comment comment keyword" style="color:#00009f;font-style:italic">@tutorial</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> destroy Destroying a Widget</span><span class="token doc-comment comment punctuation" style="color:#393A34;font-style:italic">}</span><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">.</span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token doc-comment comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"> */</span><span class="token plain"></span><br/></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">myFunction</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>如果定义了所有这些教程，并且 <code>Getting Started</code> 教程的标题是 <code>“Getting Started”</code>，则上面的示例将生成类似于以下内容的输出：</p>
<div class="language-html codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_biex"><pre class="prism-code style="color:#e3116c">tutorial-dashboard.html</span><span class="token tag attr-value punctuation" style="color:#393A34">"</span><span class="token tag punctuation"
